2a2(rgyud): byang chub sems dpa' thams cad la phyag 'tsha la lo// 'di skad bdag
2a3(rgyud): gis thos pa dus gcig na/ bcom ldan ngas ri rab kyi zom la/ 
2a4(rgyud): lha thams cad kyi mtshan mo'i gnas na/ byang chub sems dpa'abye ba khrag
2b1(rgyud): khrig 'bum phrag du ma dang thabs gcig tu bzhugs te/ de nas bcom ldan 'das lha dang lha'i bu dang / 
2b2(rgyud): lha ma yin dang / rlung lha dang / nam mkha' lding dang / klu dang / gno nga sbyin dang / mi'am ci dang
2b3(rgyud): srin po dang / rigs sngags 'chang thams cad dang / 'byung / dang / log 'dren dang / sha
2b4(rgyud): za dang snang ba dang / mi snang ba'i ma mo'i tshogs shin tu mang zhing rgya che ba dpag tshad lnga'i dkyil 'khor
2b5(rgyud): du 'dus pa sha stag dang / dge slong stong nyis brgya lnga bcus bskor cing mdun du bdar nas chos ston te
3a1(rgyud): de nas byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po lag na rdo rje/ rdo rje'i rigs thams
3a2(rgyud): cad kyis yongs su bskor cing rig pa'i tshogs dang / phyag rgya'i tshogs de dag thams cad kyis rig sngags
3a3(rgyud): 'chang bye ba phrag du mas yod/ das su bskor nas/ bcom ldan 'das dag la ba der song ste phyin nas
3a4(rgyud): bar snang las babs nas/ bcom ldan 'das kyi zhabs la mgo bos phyag 'tshal te// bcom
3a5(rgyud): ldan 'das la lan gsum bskor ba byas nas/ phyogs gcig tu 'dug pa dang / de nas bcom ldan 'das
3a6(rgyud): kyis gsang baba'i bdag po lag na rdo rje la bka' stsal pa/ gsang ba'i bdag po nyi shu rtsa lnga po 'di rnams ni nga'i
3b1(rgyud): shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i sgo yin no// oM sangs rgyas dang byang chub sems dpa' thams cad la phyag 'tshal lo// oM byang chub kyi sems
3b2(rgyud): rdo rje shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i sgo'o// oM kun tu bzang po spyod pa/ shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i sgo'o// oM yid bzhin gyi nor bu/ shes rab
3b3(rgyud): kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i sgo'o// oM 'gog pa med pa shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i sgo'o// oM skye bar 'gyur ba/ shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i sgo'o// 
3b4(rgyud): oM rnam par shes pa thams cad/ shes ra/ ba kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i sgo'o// oM 'bar ba chen/ po'i chos nyid/ shes rab kyi pha rol tu
3b5(rgyud): pa'i sgo'o// oM brtson 'grus shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i sgo'o// oM thams cad du 'gro ba shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i sgo'o// oM rdo rje thams
3b6(rgyud): cad brtan pa'i sems/ shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i sgo'o// oM de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad/ shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i sgo'o// oM
3b7(rgyud): rang bzhin rnam par dag pa'i chos nyid ye shes rnam par dag pa/ shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i sgo'o// oM las rnam par sbyong ba/ shes rab kyi
4a1(rgyud): pha rol tu phyin pa'i sgo'o// oM nges par gnod mdzes rdo rje can phaT/ shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i sgo'o// oM 'dod pa la 'dod chags
4a2(rgyud): rnam par dag pa/ shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i sgo'o// oM mgyogs pa'i rdo rje can/ shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i sgo'o// oM sU thams cad du 'gro/ 
4a3(rgyud): ba/ shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i sgo'o// oM hrIHshes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i sgo'o// oM a zhes bya ba'i sgo/ shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i sgo'o// 
4a4(rgyud): oM shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa/ shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i sgo'o// oM a ba hU/ shes rab kyi pha rol phyin pa'i sgo'o// oM e shes
4a5(rgyud): rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i sgo'o// oM de bzhi/ na gshegs pa thams cad kyi sku'i mchog/ shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i sgo/ oM de bzhin
4a6(rgyud): gshegs pa thams cad kyi gsung rnam par dag po/ shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i sgo'o// oM de bzhin ga shegs pa thams cad kyi thugs kyi rdo rje/ shes
4a7(rgyud): rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i sgo'o// bcom ldan 'das kyis de skad ces bka' stsal nas/ byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po lag na rdo rje dang / 
4a8(rgyud): thams cad dang ldan pa'i 'khor de dang / lha dang / mi dang / lha ma yin dang / dri zar bcas pa'i 'jig rten yi rangs te/ bcom ldan 'das kyis
4b1(rgyud): gsungs pa la mngon par bstod do// / 'phags pa shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i sgo nyi shu rtsa lnga pa ces bya ba/ theg pa chen po'i mdo rdzogs s+ho// / 
4b2(rgyud): rgya gar skad du/ sarba ta thA ga ta kA ya bA kut+ti gu h+ya a lang kAr b+hu ho tan+da rA dza nA ma/ bod skad du/ de bzhin gshegs pan kyi sku dang gsung dang thugs kyis gsang brgyan gyi bkod ces
4b3(rgyud): bye ba'i rgyud kyi rgyal po/ bla ma dang 'jam pa'i dbyangs kyi zhabs kyi pad+ma la gus phyag 'tshal lo// 'di skad bdag gis thos pa dus gcig na/ bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa
4b4(rgyud): thams cad kyi sku dang gsung dang thugs rdo rje ye shes rnal 'byor gyi dbang phyug chen po dang / de bzhin gsheg/ ngas pa thams cad kyi sku dang gsung dang thugs rdo rje ye shes phyag
4b5(rgyud): rgya chen po'i dam tshig byin gyis brlabs kyi rdo rje'i sku chen podang / de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sku dang gsung dang thugs rdo rje ye shes rin po che chen po'i cod pan
4b6(rgyud): gyi rtse mo'i gtsug phud kyis dbang bskur ba brnyes pa dang / de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sku dang gsung dang / thugs rdo rje ye shes kyi ting 'dzin chen po dang ldan pa dang / de bzhin gshegs/ 
4b7(rgyud): pa thams cad kyi sku dang / gsung dang thugs rdo rje ye shes kyi las sna tshogs pa chen po dang / de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sku dang gsung dang thugs rdo rje ye shes mchod pa chen po spro
4b8(rgyud): ba'i dam tshig gi gsang ba dang / de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sku dang gsung dang thugs rdo rje ye shes dkyil 'khor chen po dam tshig gi de kho na nyid/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad
5a1(rgyud): kyi sku dang gsung dang thugs rdo rje ye shes gsang ba chen po'i snying po dang / de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sku dang gsung dang thugs rdo rje ye shes kyi mnga' bdag chen
5a2(rgyud): po dang / de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sku dang gsung dang thugs rdo rje ye shes kun tu bzang po dang / de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sku dang gsung dang thugs rdo rje ye shes dpe med
5a3(rgyud): cing mi mnyam pa dang mnyam pa na mkha' lta bu dang / de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sku dang gsung dang thugs rdo rje rigs dang / snying po dang / phyag rgya dang / gsang sngags dang / rigs pa
5a4(rgyud): gnyis su med par 'gyur ba dang / de bzhin gshegs pa tham/ das cad kyi sku dang gsung dang thugs rdo rje ye shes pha rol tu phyin pa'i snying po la dga' ba dang / de bzhin gshegs pa bam/ 
5a5(rgyud): cad kyi sku dang gsung dang thugs rdo rje se shes kyi lhag pa'i snying mdzes pa dang / de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad sku dang gsung dang thugs rdo rje ye shes rgyan chen po bkod pa'i
5a6(rgyud): dkyil 'khor chen po'i snying po la na mkha'i khams thams cad kyi rdul phra rab kyi rdul dang mnyam pa'i rdo rje ye shes chen po 'ba' zhig dang thabs gcig tu bzhug so// de'ang 'di lta ste/ sgo
5a7(rgyud): mtha' yas pa zhes bya ba'i rdo rje yum chen mo dang / na mkha' sgo zhes bya ba'i rdo rje yum chen mo dang / a bo dza'i sgo zhes bya ba'i rdo rje yum chen mo dang / 'gyur ba med pa'i sgo zhes bya ba'i rdo rje
5a8(rgyud): yum chen mo dang / shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin ma zhes bya ba'i rdo rje yum chen mo dang / gzhan yang ma lus shing lus pa med pa'i 'jig rten gyi khams kyi rdul phra rab dang mnyam pa'i brtson
5b1(rgyud): 'grus dang ldan pa'i rdo rje btsun mo stong phrag brgya la'ang 'di lta ste/ mda'i mtshon cha'i lag ces bya ba'i rdo rje btsun mo dang / dbang phyug la lta ba'i rim zhes bya ba'i rdo rje btsun mo dang / nye ba
5b2(rgyud): zhi ba'i rang bzhin ras zhes bya ba'i rdo rje btsun mo dang / gyen du lta ba'i bzhin ras zhes bya ba'i rdo rje btsun mo dang / 'dod zla mtshan rdo rje zhes bya ba'i rdo rje btsun mo dang / brda' sprod pa ma zhes bya ba'i
5b3(rgyud): rdo rje btsun mo dang / 'bri ba'i sgo zhes bya ba'i rdo rje btsun mo dang / rol pa dang ldan pa zhes bya ba'i rdo rje btsun mo dang / 'dod pa'i mchog ces bya ba'i rdo rje btsun mo dang / dbang phyug gis bde ba'i/ 
5b4(rgyud): sgo zhes bya ba'i rdo rje btsun mo dang / dmigs pa'i sgo zhes bya ba nga'i rdo rje btsun mo dang / brang las skyes zhes bya ba'i rdorjebatsun mo ste/ de dag la sogs pa rdo rje btsun mo rnams kyis
5b5(rgyud): yongasu bskor cing mdun du bdar to// gzhan yang dpag tu med/ pa'i rdo rje pho nya mo chen mo rnams dang / thabs gcig/ tu bzhugs te/ de yang 'di lta ste/ snying bskul bar byed pa
5b6(rgyud): zhes bya ba'i rdo rje pho nya mo chen mo dang / gdug pa thams cad 'gugs pa zhes bya ba'i rdo rje pho nya mo chen mo dang / rje su mnyes pa rdo rje zhes bya ba'i rdo rje pho nya mo chen mo dang / khrag 'gugs pa zhes/ 
5b7(rgyud): bya ba'i rdo rje pho nya mo chen mo dang / thams cad 'phrog pa zhes bya ba'i rdo rje po nya mo chen mo la sogs pa'o// gzhan yang 'jig rten gyi khams rgyas pa'i rdo rje sgo srung ma chen mo rnams dang / 
5b8(rgyud): yang thabs gcig ste/ de'ang 'di lta ste/ rdo rje 'bebs pa zhes bya ba zhi rje sgo srung ma chen mo dang / dam tshig gsum ldan ces bya ba'i rdo rje sgo srung ma chen mo dang / 'jig pa'i yan lag can ces
6a1(rgyud): bya ba'i rdo rje sgo srung ma chen mo dang / thog ma pa zhes bya ba'i rdo rje sgo srung ma chen mo dang / gdul dka' 'dul ces bya ba'i rdo rje sgo srung ma chen mo la sogs pa'o// gzhan
6a2(rgyud): yang mi mnyam dang mnyam pa'i rdo rje bran mo chen mo rnams dang / yang thabs gcig ste/ de'ang 'di lta ste/ sku gsung thugs thams cad rdo rje 'ching ba ma zhes bya ba'i rdo rje bran mo chen mo dang / 'jigs
6a3(rgyud): pa'i me'i gdong zhes bya ba'i rdo rje bran mo chen mo dang / gtsigs shing rnam par 'gyur ba'i gdong zhes bya ba'i rdo rje bran mo chen mo dang / 'jig rten gsum 'ching ba zhes bya ba rdo rje bran mo chen mo dang / 
6a4(rgyud): bskal bar gnas pa zhes bya ba la sogs pa'i rdo rje bran mtshan/ me'o// gzhan yang dpe med pa'i rdo rje rol ba chen ma rnams dang yang thabs gcig ste/ de'ang 'di lta ste/ de bzhin
6a5(rgyud): gshegs pa thams cad kyi sku gsung thugs rdo rje dgyes pa zhesaba'i rdo rje rol pa chen mo dang / kun nas 'bebs pa zhen/ bya ba'i rdo rje rol pa chen mo dang / 'jig rten gsum rab tu 'joms
6a6(rgyud): pa zhes bya ba'i rdo rje rol pa chen mo dang / rab tu dga' ba'i rjesu 'gro ba zhes bya ba'i rdo rje rol pa chen mo dang / thams cad dga' bar byed pa zhes bya ba'i rdo rje rol pa chen mo la sogs pa'o// gzhan yang
6a7(rgyud): namakha'i khams thams cad rgyas par gang ba'i rdo rje'i yab rnams dang yang thabs gcig ste/ de'ang 'di lta ste/ 'dod pa'i dbang phyug ces bya ba'i rdo rje yab chen po dang / mkha' 'gro'i rdo rjes dbang
6a8(rgyud): phyag dang / dri la dbang phyug dang / stug po bkod pa dang / zla ba'i 'od dang / 'dun pa srel dang / skye ba yongasu dor ba dang / legs par sbyangs pa dang / 'dod pa'i rdo rje dang / gdung ba bskyed pa dang / 'dul
6b1(rgyud): bar byed pa dang / gdug pa thams cad sel bar byed pa dang / de kho na nyid kyi mgon po dang / gnas pa po dang / brtse ba can dang / chos 'chang dang / bskyod pa po dang / spong ba po dang / 'ching ba po dang / 
6b2(rgyud): skor ba po dang / de dag la sogs pa rdo rje yab rnams so// gzhan yang mtha' yas pa'i rdo rje pho nya mo 'phrog pa'i rdo rje bran po rdo rje'i tshogs dang thabs gcig ste/ de'ang 'di lta ste/ rdo rje rlung zhes bya ba
6b3(rgyud): dang rdo rje me dang / rdo rje mi 'khrugs pa dang / rdo rje chu dang / gzhan yang rdo rje rgyal po chen po bzhi la 'di lta ste/ zhi bar byed pa dang / rgyas par byed pa dang / dbang du byed pa dang / mi shes pa thams/ 
6b4(rgyud): cad zad par byed pa ste de dag la sogs pa'o// gzhan yang mcho ga tu rgya chen po sangs rgyas kyi ye shes rab tu gnas ngapa'i mchod pa dang ldan pa bcom ldan 'das ston pa rtag pa mchog/ 
6b5(rgyud): gi mnga' bdag ste/ kun tu bzang po'i sku yis ni// 'jig rte/ na gsum gyi dkyil 'khor spros// bcom ldan rdo rje 'dzin legs bzhugs// gsang ba rgyan gyi sbyor bas so// de
6b6(rgyud): nas de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad bskyed par byed pa'i yum gsang ba'i rdo rje 'dus pa thob ste/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi yab dang lhan cig tu dga' ba'i bde ba rje su byung ste/ 
6b7(rgyud): 'khor dang bcas pa rnams bcom ldan 'das kyi spyan sngar lhags te/ rdo rje'i glu 'dis mngon par bstod nas zhu ba zhus pa/ sangs rgyas kun don khyod phyag 'tshal// rdo rje 'byung ba khyod la 'dud// 
6b8(rgyud): thugs kyi rin chen mchog khyod 'dud// chos kyi blo gros khyod la 'dud// chos rnams kun mchog khyod la 'dud// sna tshogs dgongs pa khyod la 'dud// dam tshig mchog gi khyod la 'dud// rdo rje sems
7a1(rgyud): dpa' phyag 'tshal 'dud// grags pa chen po bdag cag ni// mgon po khyod la zhu ba zhu// sangs rgyas thams cad bskyed byed yum// dkyil 'khor gyi ni dkyil 'khor mchog
7a2(rgyud): de nas bcom ldan 'das rdo rje sems dpa' des de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi rdo rje'i yum rnams la 'di skad ces bka' stsal to// de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi yum rnams de skad
7a3(rgyud): ma smra gcig/ 'jig rten thams cad la khyab pa'i dkyil 'khor gyi rgyal po chen po 'di la ma 'ongs pa'i sems can rnams dad par mi 'gyur zhing / rang gi sems yongasu sun 'byin la de ma
7a4(rgyud): mthong ba'i chos la ma dad pas rang gi sems yang dag par su nu phyung ste/ mnar med pa rnams su skyes nas bskal pa stong phrag mang por mnar med pa'i sdug bsngal rjesu 'byung bar
7a5(rgyud): 'gyuraro// de rgya lam na mnar med pa'i sdug bsngal las grol/ te/ mi rnamasu skyes par gyur kyang rnam par 'gyur/ ba'i bzhin du 'gyuraro// rjed dngas po rnams dang / blo gros chung
7a6(rgyud): ba rnams dang / khyi dang / bya rog dang / byi la dang / phag dang / stog dang / glang po che dang / seng ge'i nga ro 'dra ba dag tu 'gyuraro// de dang 'dre bar mi bya zhing blta bar mi bya'o// de nas de bzhin gshegs
7a7(rgyud): pa thams cad bskyed pa'i yum de rnams kyis bcom ldan 'das la 'di skad ces gsol to// bcom ldan 'das ji ltar sems can de rnams kyi mnar med pa'i sdug bsngal zad par 'gyur// 
7a8(rgyud): bcom ldan 'das kyis bka' stsal pa/ gang gis 'di'i ming gzung nas yongs su zad par 'gyuraro// bsod nams de'i rgyus de'i las kyi sgrib pa zad de bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang
7b1(rgyud): chub kyi skal pa can du 'gyur ro// de nas de dag yid dga' ba skyes nas yang bcom ldan 'das la 'di skad ces gsol to// bcom ldan 'das bstan du gsol/ bsod nams dang ye shes kyi cho ga
7b2(rgyud): kyi rgyus dkyil 'khor chen po'i rgyal po sems can thams cad la phan pa dang bde ba'i phyir gang ma 'ongs pa'i sems can rnams kyis dran pa tsam gyis sangs rgyas kyi byang chub thob par 'gyuraro// 
7b3(rgyud): de nas bcom ldan 'das kyis kun tu bzang po chen po 'od 'phro ba gsang ba rdo rje zhes bya ba'i ting 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs so// rang gi sku dang gsung dang thugs rdo rje rnams la de bzhin gshegs
7b4(rgyud): ba thams cad kyi sku'i dam pa 'di bka' stsal pa/ dkyila'akhor kun gyis yum gyur pa// stong nyid ye shes nyid du bshad// ci zhig nga yis bstan par bya// rtogs pa
7b5(rgyud): thams cad rnam par spangs// sems can rnams la phan bzhed pa// gang zhig cung zad bstan par bya// de kun sgyu mas sgyu ma'o// 'gro ba sgyu ma lta bur shes// de nas sgyu ma
7b6(rgyud): lta bu yis// sgyu ma lta bu'i dkyil 'khor bya// nam mkha'i khams kyis khyab pa yis// thams cad yum gyis yang dag 'khrugs// phyi rol yang ni brtag par bya// gas pa'i dkyil 'khor yum
7b7(rgyud): rnams kyis// dben zhing dga' ba'i gan su ni// yid kyi legs par 'dus byas pa// na mkha' la ni thig gis gdab// thog mar de yi dam pas so// de nas rnal 'byor chen pos thig/ 
7b8(rgyud): gsang ba'i yum gyi dkyil 'khor ro// mu khyud dag gi rnam bdun du// kun nas yongasu bskor bar bya// dbus kyis cha ru dkyil 'khor ni// 'khor lo lta bur bri bar bya// kun nas brgyad gzhi
8a1(rgyud): mdzes pa ni// dkyil 'khor bzhi yi dbus su'o// 'khor lo'i lte ba'i dbus su ni// pad+ma ze 'bru ldan pa bri// mtshams dang mtsham su 'dab ma ni// ji lta ba bzhin bsnyes/ 
8a2(rgyud): bcas pas// srad bu lnga yis yang dag 'khrugs// srad bu bzhi yis nye bar spras// sgo bzhi dang ni yang dag ldan// rta babs seng ge dag gis brgyan// gdugs dang rgyal mtshan ba dan sogs/ 
8a3(rgyud): bla res steng du bres pa dang // rin chen rdo rje bang ldan sngon// dpag bsam shing gi lcug mas khyab// bum bzang rin chen ldan pa'i mchog/ rgyan phreng glang po ldan pa'i ni// phyi rol gnas te
8a4(rgyud): legs par bri// rtog dang mi rtog rnam spangs te// dkyil 'kho dar chen po'i dbus su ni// gsang ba rgyan gyi rdo rje bya// mnyam par gzhag cing spro ba yis// sems kyis bri ba nyid
8a5(rgyud): bya// de nas lha mo zhal bzhi ma// shes rab pha rol phyin dang/ kha// phyag bzhi pa la spyan yangs ma// phyag gnyis kyis ni chos 'chad cing // zhi ba'i g.yas par rdo rje ste// g.yon
8a6(rgyud): pa pad+mas rnam par brgyan// dkar dang dmar po cher sngo ba// sngo bsangs rin chen mchog mdzes 'od// gtsug na rin chen gtsug tor che// gtsug rgyan cod pan daM pa can// skal pa chen po
8a7(rgyud): 'od ldan ma// rgyan rnams kun gyis rnam par klubs// gos kyis lto ni legs bsgribs pa// bzhin gyi dkyil 'khor 'dzum bcas shing // sna tshogs gis ni legs gyon pa// dbu ma'i zhal
8a8(rgyud): ras gser gyi 'od// zhabs gnyis dbus 'khor lo ste// mdun na rin chen bdun gnas pa// pad+ma mchog ldan sang+ge'i khri// zla ba rdo rje 'dzin pa'i gdan// nyi ma'i dkyil 'khor 'od 'phro ba/ 
8b1(rgyud): rgyab du nyi ma'i dkyil 'khor ni// dpa' bo de yis bri bar bya// 'di yi mdun du bri bya ba// dpa' bo mtha' yas pa yis zhal// stong phrag du ma'i phyag ldan ma// mtshan nyid thams cad yang dag
8b2(rgyud): rdzogs// rgyan rnams kun gyis rnam par brgyan// phyag gi rdo rje pad+ma 'chang // sna tshogs phyag rgyas phyag gzhan dkrigs// gtsug ldan dar gyi cod pan can// dbu brgyan pad+ma'i bzhin ras ma
8b3(rgyud): zla ba'i dkyil 'khor dag la bzhugs// de 'od nyi ma lta bu'i 'od// dpa' bo'i rnal 'byor ldan pa yi// dpa' bo des ni bri bar bya// rdo rje sems dpa' bdag bsgom te// der ni snyems pas
8b4(rgyud): 'gro bar bya// dpa' bos lho ru br-i bya ba// gshin rje'i 'dab ma mdzes pa la// mchog sbyin na mkha' dge ma yang / rin chen khril legs par bzhugs// bzhin ras sngo la spyan
8b5(rgyud): dkar ba// 'dzum bcas nor bu'i 'og bag can// mgul rgyan rin chen phreng ba mchog/ rkang gdub gdu bu rin po che// yid bzhin nor bu'i lag pa can// sbyin pa'i pha rol phyin dgod/ 
8b6(rgyud): nam// de nas blo ldan rab song ste// nub tu yang ni de bzhin du// dpal dang ldan pas legs par bri// chu las skyes ma yid 'phrog ma// dmar po'i gos 'dzin dag pa ma// gtsug na cod pan gyis spras ma// sbrul
8b7(rgyud): rgyan sna tshogs lus can ma// dar dang rin chen gyis klubs na// pad+ma 'byed pa'i sbyor ba yis// phyag gi lo 'dab dang ldan pas// zla ba'i gdan la yang dag bzhugs// nyi ma du ma'i snang ba can// ji ltar rigs
8b8(rgyud): ba bri bar bya// de nas byang du phyin na su// song ste dpa' bos bri bya ba// mi g.yo bzhin ras grags chen ma// mar gad 'bar ba mtshungs pa mo// dkar po'i dar gyis yang dag klubs// gtsug na nor bu cod
9a1(rgyud): ban bzang // gtsug rgyan sna tshogs dag gis spras// rdo rje dril bu'i lag bkram// sna tshogs rgyan dang gos ldan pas// zla ba'i gdan la yang dag bzhugs// 'od
9a2(rgyud): kyis gtams pa'i dkyil 'khor mchog/ de nas 'tshams kyi 'dab ma la// me tog gdug pa dri ldan ma// rdo rje snang byed dag pa ma// mchod pa sngags rig pa yis bris// gzugs sgra dri dang
9a3(rgyud): dang reg/ rang gi bdag po'i phyog su'o// 'dab ma 'dab mar thams cad du// bzhad dang sgeg dang dbyangs chen mo// gar gyi phyag rgya grags chen po// sngags pas 'bad de bri bar bya// pad+ma la
9a4(rgyud): skyes 'dab ma la// thams cad du ni 'grub pa bri// skra rnams dag ni thams cad la//  sbyong ba ni rnam pazhi dang / phyi rol du yang stsal sogs// mngan yang dag thob bya/ 
9a5(rgyud): de nas khrus byas lus byugs la// me tog gdug sogs kyi/ bdug ste// sna tshogs gis ni rab gyen la// me tog rwa nga dang gis kyis brgyan// gtsug phud cod pan dang ldan
9a6(rgyud): zhing // mdzes pa'i dar gyis yang dag klubs// rdo rje dril bu lag par ldan// sbyor ba bzang ba'i rnam gzhag gis// de nas thams cad dgug par bya// rdo rje ma mo dka' thub che// bzlog
9a7(rgyud): dang rnal ma'i phyag rgya yis// rdo rje sems dpa' bzlas nas su// rdo rje'i sbyor bas gar bya zhing // lan gsum du ni g.yas bskor bas// rdo rje ma me'i dkyil 'khor rnams// dam
9a8(rgyud): tshig ldan pa thams cad byon// klu dbyangs kyis ni rgyal pos bskul// rang gi slob ma'i tshigs gar gyis// dregs pa yis ni g.yas dang g.yon// 'gying ba dang ni 'dud par bya// 'dir
9b1(rgyud): gshegs 'dir shegs sems can don mdzad brtson pa po// ser sna mi mnga' sangs rgyas tshogs mchog mtha' dag dang // bde gshegs dam pa'i yum gyur srid pa'i bskyed pa po// pha
9b2(rgyud): rol don mdzad dus la di ring bab pa lags// ces so de nas de dag rang nyid kyis// rdzu 'phrul rnam par 'phrul pas byon// mtshan ma dag ni bzang po rnams// dkyil 'khor dag tu blta bar bya// 
9b3(rgyud): rang ngam gzhan la bab sogs pa'i// mtshan ma ji ltar mthong ba na// de tshe nges par ma mo ni// bde gshegs thugs kyi dgongs par byon// de nas mchod yon zhabs bsil cho ga ji bzhin
9b4(rgyud): rab brtags te// de tshe babs pa'i sems can bsod nams da ldan la bri bar bya// gal te de ni mi smra ba na hUM gi yi dge dang // ldan pa'i glu dbyangs kyis ni yongs su bskul ba
9b5(rgyud): nyid du bya// de nas shes rab ldan ma bzhugs// slob ma'i gtso bo thal sbyar te// mig la mig dar gyis g.yog/ sa la// rab dga' bdag yin yang dag dga'// ma mo
9b6(rgyud): thams cad la dmigs te// der ni me tog dor bar bya// me tog gang la lhung gyur pa// ma mo de ni de yis 'grub// de nas go rims ji bzhin du// sgo skyong ba nas brtsams nas su// 
9b7(rgyud): shes rab pha rol phyin pa'i bar// slob ma la ni bshad par bya// dam tshig thob par gyur nas su// sdom pa dag ni bzung bar bya// ma mo'i sngags dang phyag rgya ni// mnyam par gzhag
9b8(rgyud): pas bstan par bya// gzhan du slob dpon blo ngan ni// nges par dmyal bar 'dod par 'gyur// des kyang yang dag de 'grub cing // myur du dmyal bar 'gro bar 'gyur// bgegs dang
10a1(rgyud): log par 'dren pa 'am// rims dang gdon dang dug sogs kyis// gdungs te nad kyis rgyun du ni// 'chi ba ru yang 'gyur ba yin// rdo rje slob dpon smad pa na// 
10a2(rgyud): rtag tu dmyal ba nyid du ni// rab tu spongs pa'i slob ma 'gro// mkha' las rdo rje ji bzhin no// des na bu kye dam tshig ni// khyod kyis rtag tu srung bar byos// ma mo kun gyi sdom pa ni/ 
10a3(rgyud): theg pa chen po'i tshogs gnas// de nas yang bcom ldan 'das kyis ting 'dzin la bzhugs te/ rdo rje 'dzin pa thams cad kyis yum rnams kyi dam tshig la bka' stsal pa/ rin chen sems kyi
10a4(rgyud): dam tshig gis// rnam pa gsum ni sbyang bar bya// thog mtha' dbar gyi sbyor ba yis// chung 'bring mchog gi dbye ba yis// de 'dra'i dam tshig yang dag pa// sangs rgyas kun gyi
10a5(rgyud): bka' stsal to// ji srid sems ni sbyangs kyi bar// 'bad pa yis ni bsgom par bya// bud med thams cad mthong ba ni// lan gsum du ni bskor nas kyang // spyi bor phyag ni
10a6(rgyud): byas nas su// lan gsum bar du gsol ba btab// bdag gi ma khyod bu yin te// ji srid byang chub thob bar du// byang chub yan lag nu ma la// byung ma rang gi 'o mas skyongs// de nas sbyor ldan
10a7(rgyud): rab dge ba'i// dbang bskur ba ni sbyin par bya// gser la sogs pa'i bum pa ru// dri yis chu yi yongs bkang la// dar dang ras sogs gis g.yogs te// me tog chun pos mgul
10a8(rgyud): rgyan nas// rin rin sman gyis rab bkang ba'i// gcig lhag bcu drug bzang ba la// ma mo'i snying po nyid kyis ni// brgya rtsa brgyad du bzlas pa yis// sngags shes pas ni dbang bskur ro// 
10b1(rgyud): slob ma zhi ba bzang po yis// thog mar zhu ba byas nas kyang // zhabs gnyis la ni mgos btud nas// bdag ni che ge mo rdo rje// byang chub sems ni rnam sgom pa'o// slob dpon zhabs kyi chu
10b2(rgyud): skyes la// dbang bskur phyir ni zhu ba bgyid// bskal pa chen po bdag la stsol// slob dpon mchog tu rmad byung ba// dbang bskur ba rgyal ba thams cad kyi// sangs rgyas byang chub rab sgrub pa/ 
10b3(rgyud): des ni bdag gi sems can rnams// don gyi dam pa bdag gis bgyi// sangs rgyas kun gyi don bgyid pa// brtul zhugs bzang po khyod kyi drin// de nas dbang bskur sbyor ba yis// rdo rje sems/ 
10b4(rgyud): dpa'i go 'phang gnas// slob ma ye shes rdo rje yi// go 'pha rangs la ni bzhag nas su// bum pa bzang po gcig/ dag ma ni// yang na bcu drug dag gam ni// lnga 'am yang na
10b5(rgyud): bcu yis ni// dkyil 'khor du ni dbang bskur ro// dkyil 'khor gyi mdun du ni// dkyil 'khor pad+ma dra bar bya// pad+ma lo 'dab brgyad pa la// gser lte ba
10b6(rgyud): ldan pa bri// de yi dbus su rdo rje bri// sna tshogs rdo rje 'od zer phreng // de yi mdun du 'khor lo bri// chen po rin chen bdun gyis bskor// lho yi phyogs su rin po che// nub tu pad+ma nyid
10b7(rgyud): yin te// byang du ral gri chen po'o// 'bar ba'i phreng 'khrugs 'od zer can// gra yi phyogs ni thams cad du// me tog bdug pa dri zhim pa// 'od ldan pa ni skal ba che// sgo dang sgo ru
10b8(rgyud): bzhi nyid do// phyi rol du yang mi 'chi kun// gcig nas gcig tu rgyal sgrogs pa// bde byed gcer bu'i cha lugs te// ming thos pa dang ldan pa'o// dkyil 'khor de yi dbus su ni// slob
11a1(rgyud): ma bsnyems dang bcas pa bzhag/ chos kyi rang bzhin gtam brjod de// de ring khyod ni rigs su skyes// 'khor los bsgyur ba'i rgyal po chen// rtag pa dam pa'i dbang
11a2(rgyud): byug pa// thabs dang shes rab ldan pa'i dpal// dag pa'i dbang phyug kun gyi bdag/ rdo rje pad+ma lag byin te// gnang ba bzang po rab tu sbyin// bu yis bya ba chen po gyis// sangs rgyas kun
11a3(rgyud): gyi go 'phangs gnas// der ni sbyor ba 'ongs nas su// gsang ba'i sdom pa sbyin par bya// 'di ni mchog tu dga' ba ste// yum rnams rab tu rmad byung ba'o// dus su 'dod pa nyid du
11a4(rgyud): gyis// dam tshig mchog tu gyur pa'o// brtul zhugs bzang dbus ci 'byor pas// de nas yon ni phul byas nas/ slob dpon gyi ni zhabs la btud// ma dang chung ma bu mo dang / 
11a5(rgyud): sring mo sring mo'i bu mo dang // bu rnams dang ni bdag nyid dang // rgyal po longs spyod gter dang ni// nor dang / 'bru dang grong shing rta// glang po rta dang ba glang sogs// ma
11a6(rgyud): he dang ni ma he mo// gzhan dang gzhan yang ci 'dod pa// bla ma la ni chen pos dbus// bya dang mi bya rdzas kyi mchog/ thams cad kyang ni dbul bar bya// de nas bcom ldan mi rnams la// 
11a7(rgyud): rgyan phreng rnams dang bzhad gad dang // sgeg dang rtse 'jo dga' ba dang // rab tu dga' ba'i bde chen dang // gza' btung bca' ba la sogs pa// rnam pa du ma thams cad kyis// mchod nas
11a8(rgyud): gshegs su gsol bar bya// sems can kun gyi don dang ni// bdag gi yang ni cher ches mdzad// bde gshegs gang du gshegs pa der// ma mo thams cad gshegs su gsol// 
11b1(rgyud): shes rab ldan pas yon phul te// slob ma'i mchog dang bcas pa yis// gar byas lag pa mgor bzhag ste// rims kyis 'gyed dang 'dud par bya// de nas bzang mo rnam gnyis te/ 
11b2(rgyud): thams cad sgrub par byed pa'i mchog/ bdag gi skal bzang stsal nas kyang // rang gi sras kyi gnas su gshegs// de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sku dang gsung dang thugs
11b3(rgyud): rdo rje ye shes yum chen mo rnams kyi phyag rgya ye shes kyi dkyil 'khor yongasu rdzogs s+ho// / de nas de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi gsang ba'i yum bcom ldan

11b6(rgyud): ba// rdo rje sku ste rdo rje mchog/ dngos grub kun gyi bde ster ba// rdo rje chen po gsung du gsol// thugs kyi rin chen ldan pa'i mchog/ gzi brjid rdo rje snang ba can// sems can rnams
11b7(rgyud): kyi rdzu 'phrul dang // 'grub pa'i yon tan 'byung gnas gsungs// sangs rgyas kun gyi rnal 'byor che// rnal 'byor chen po dbang phyug che// dpa' bo'i sbyor bas gar gnas pa'i// dpa'
11b8(rgyud): po chen pos bshad du gsol// las kun gyis ni 'bras brnyes pas// sna tshogs mkhyen pa dbang phyug che// sems can rnams kyi yab chen po// sna tshogs dam pas bshad du gsol// 
12a1(rgyud): zhes bya bas so// de nas bcom ldan rtag pa'i rgyal// dam pa'i dbang phyug kun mkhyen pas// gsung mchog na mkha' dang mtshungs pa'i// zab mo yi ni chos bka'
12a2(rgyud): stsa la la 'di na sgrub po gang yang med// dngos grub bam ni sgrub thabs kyang // thams cad rnam par rtog las byung // rnam rtog kyang ni dmigs ma yin// bdag med sangs rgyas rnams kyang
12a3(rgyud): med 'chos rnams med cing chos nyid med// sbyor ba med cing sems can med// de bzhin pa dang ma yang med// byed pa med cing skyong ba med// 'bras bu med cing rgyu yod min// longs spyod med cing / 
12a4(rgyud): zab bo med// shes med shes pa po yang med// rnam shes/ med cing shes bya med// brdzun min bden pa'ang ma yin pa// des na snang ba thams cad ni// sgyu ma lta bu nyid
12a5(rgyud): las byung // de ltar chos rnams rnams rig na// grol nas go/ sa par mi 'gyur te// dngos grub chen po 'grub par 'gyur// sangs rgyas byang chub bde chen po// zab mo'i chos
12a6(rgyud): ni thos pa na// mkhas pa gang zhig dad gyur na// snying po'i phyag rgya sngags rig rnams// gdon mi za bar 'grub par 'gyur// sbyor ba 'di ni bcom ldan gsungs// thams cad dag
12a7(rgyud): par byed pa'i mchog/ gsang ba'i rgyan la legs bzhugs nas// sems can rnams la bstan pa po// de nas yum rnams tshim gyur te// rang byung ba la zhu ba zhus// grub pa'i sgrub thabs/ 
12a8(rgyud): rab sbyar ba// mnga' bdag rnal 'byor rnams kyis gsungs// de nas yang bcom ldan 'das kyis de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyis yum las kyi dam tshig 'byung ba rdo rje zhes bya ba'i ting
12b1(rgyud): 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs nas 'di skad ces bka' stsal to// nam mkha'i dkyil 'khor bsgom par bya// de yi steng du ma nyams pa// na mkha'i mtha' klas khyab pa yi// phyogs kun tu ni rab
12b2(rgyud): 'phro ba'o// de yi steng du gzi brjid che// dus mtha'i me dang mtshungs 'dra ba// de yi steng du sa chen po// gser gyi ri bo dang mtshungs pa// de yi steng du chur shes bya// zla ba gang ba kha ba 'dra/ 
12b3(rgyud): sngags pas cho ga bzhin du bsam// rin chen bzhi yi rang bzhin bzang // stong phrag brgyad cu rtsa bzhi yi// dpag tshad kyi ni tshad tsam pa// gru bzhi pa la sgo bzhi pa// rta babs bzhi yi
12b4(rgyud): rtse mo can// ri bo chen po cog brgyad pa// dbus bu rdo rje'i nga ri bo mchog/ de yi steng du rdo rje che// kun tu phyogangs pa yongs su bsgom// sngo bsangs mar ga ta 'dra ba// 
12b5(rgyud): sna tshogs 'od kyis yang dag 'khrugs// de yi steng du rdo rje/ che// rtse mo lnga pa rnam par bsam// dkar po she la dang 'dra ba po// 'od zer lnga yis rnam par spras/ 
12b6(rgyud): de yi steng du rin po che// chu skyes sngon po'i 'dab 'dra ba// sna tshogs 'od zer stong gi phreng // phyogs bcu na mkha' khyab pa'o// de yi gtsug tu pad+ma che// na mkha' khyab pa yi ni mchog/ 
12b7(rgyud): lo ma stong phrag du ma can// lte ba dang ni ze 'brus dkrigs// de yi mdun du nyi ma che// 'od zer stong phrag du ma can// de yi steng du zla ba che// dkar po'i 'od zer 'bar bas bkrigs/ 
12b8(rgyud): nam mkha'i khams ni gang ba yin// gzi brjid dkar po 'phro ba'o// de yi dbus su ma mo bri// dus gsum bzhugs pa'i sangs rgyas kyang // yongasu dag pa mkha' 'dra ma// zla ba'i
13a1(rgyud): dkyil 'khor 'phro ba mo// phyag gnyis ma la thugs zhi ba// bsam gtan spyan ldan bsam gtan yid// bsam gtan mchog gi phyag rgya yi// ser mo gzhon nu
13a2(rgyud): rab bshad pa// dkar po'i gos 'dzin mdzes pa mo// dkar po yi ni rgyan gyis brgyan// ral pa'i thor tshugs cod pan bzang // gtsug gi nor bu 'od ldan pa// ye shes gdan la
13a3(rgyud): mnyam par bzhugs// ba spu rnams kyi rtse bu gnas// rgyal ba rab tu 'bros pa ste// byang chub pha rol son par mdzad// de yi thugs kar rnam bsam pa// yi ge mchog tu mi 'gyur
13a4(rgyud): ba/ yi ge rnams kyis yang dag dkrigs// thams cad du ni legs 'phro ba'o// sangs rgyas rnams ni mdun gnas pa// rab tu thal mo sbyor ba'o// de bzhin byang chub
13a5(rgyud): sems dpa' rnams// rigs sngags khro bo'i tshigs rnam sa ni// chos nyan pa yi tshul du yang // dkyil 'khor du ni bzhag par bya// sgo yi phyogs ni thams cad du// ske
13a6(rgyud): skyong ba ni bzhi rnams so// sbyin pa la sogs ci rigs par// bcu drug po'ang bzhag par bya// me tog bdug pa mar me che// ji lta ba bzhin bzhag par bya// lha klu de bzhin gnod sbyin
13a7(rgyud): dang // dri za lha min dmyal las byung // 'di rnams thams cad lhun po la// kun nas yongasu bzhag par bya// de nas me tog phreng ldan 'jug/ dri dang me tog yang dag ldan// gos dkar
13a8(rgyud): 'dzin pa dpal dang ldan// rgyan rnams kun gyis rnam par brgyan// shes rab 'phro dang lhan cig tu// rdo rje sems dpa' rjes dran pa// bdag pas de ni dag par bya// shes rab sbyor bas
13b1(rgyud): gang gnas pas// sgo yi drung du legs 'khod la// glu 'di yis ni spyan drang bya// thugs rje mnga' ba chos kyi dbang phyug sangs rgyas yum// rang gi yab kyi tshogs dang sras dang bcas te byon//

13b3(rgyud): yi ge bde bar gshegs pas rjes bskos pas// mkha' ltar yongs dag dri med dam bca' dran par mdzod// ma mo rnams ni mchog glus bskul bas byon par 'gyur// de nas bcom
13b4(rgyud): ldan 'das ma byon par mthong nas rang gis me tog gi snyim pa dang mchod yon dang zhabs sil dbul bar bya'o// oM bdag gi mchod yon zhabs bsil 'di// ci bde bar ni bzhesu
13b5(rgyud): gsol// de nas de dang lhan cig tu// 'dres pa ru ni gyur/ bar bsam// oM sarba ta thA ga ta pradz+nyA dz+nyA na sa ma ye hUM/ sa ma ya s+t+waM/ de nas 'di yis brtan par bya ste/ oM sarba ta
13b6(rgyud): bA ga ta tsa la sa ma ye ma tsa la s+t+waM/ de nas 'dis mnyes par bya/ oM sarba ta thA ga ta/ ma na san+na sti sa ma yaM hUM/ e h+ye hi dza e h+ye hi dzaHde nas dpag tu med pa'i ngo mtshar chen po lta ba'i
13b7(rgyud): phyir/ oM sarba a ga puN+Da ri ma hA b+ha ga bAn sa le sma ra sma ra s+pha ra s+pha ra sarba a ga a bA yu biSh+Ta ma hA bud+d+ha sa mu dran hUM hUM aM/ 'di yis ma mo bskul nas su// sangs rgyas sprin ni 'od po che// 
13b8(rgyud): dkyil 'khor ba la spro bar bya// de nas gsang sngags 'di yi ni// bsngags te me tog dor bar bya// oM sarba a ga puN+Da ri pra tIts+tsha d+hi ku su ma a dza li hUM aHde nas ji ltar bshad pa bzhin du
14a1(rgyud): dkyil 'khor gyi bum pa rnams la rig sngags 'dis ji ltar bshad pa ltar legs par byin gyis brlabs la rang gis dbang bskur rang gi snying po rang gis blang bar bya'o// 
14a2(rgyud): de nas las thams cad kyi nus pa dang ldan pa dang / dngos grub thams cad 'grub par 'gyur ro// de nas me tog la sogs dang // bza' dang btung dang ro dag gis// mchod la sngon gyi rim
14a3(rgyud): ba bzhin// slob ma'i rgyal po gzhug par bya// 'khor los bsgyur ba'i rim pa yi// sbyor ba yis ni dbang bskur ro// rdo rje rin chen de bzhin pad// las kyi rdo rje de bzhin no// zhags
14a4(rgyud): pa lcags kyu dril bu dang // lcags sgrog rnga yab dang ni ga dugs// ral gri mig sman thur ma gnyis// rgyal po'i nye bar spyod pa dang // de la rgyan rnams brtan nas su//

14a6(rgyud): gzhug/ zhi ba dang ni rgyas pa'i las// dbang dang drag shul spyod pa ni// legs par rnam par dag sems kyis// ci 'dod par ni bya ba byos// las rnams kun gyi 'bras bu yang // sbyor
14a7(rgyud): ba 'di yis 'grub par 'gyur// de nas bcom ldan 'das rdo rje sems dpa' chen pos slar yang las dam pa rgyas par bkod pa zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs nas 'di skad
14a8(rgyud): ces bka' stsal to// ji ltar gzugs kyi snod byas la// dkyil 'khor gyis ni dbus su bzhag/ zho dang mar srar 'o ma ni// tsan dan dmar po dang bsres te// ga pur dang ni ldan byas la/ 
14b1(rgyud): yid la byed pas bzlas te sgrub// zla ba nyi ma gzas bzung che// sbyor ba bzang po'i rnam bzhag bya// thog mar me ni spar byas nas// 'bad pa yis ni rlung gi bu// gser gyi snod du bsdu bar bya// 
14b2(rgyud): ba ru na yi khu bas sbyar// nyi ma dang ni zla ba la// slar yang rdzas de bskam par bya// de nas lho ru lha mo yi// khrag dang sa bon blugs par bya// de yis myur du rdzas dag ni// 'grub par 'gyur
14b3(rgyud): the tsom med// grub nas thog mar lha mo la// cung zad tsam cig dbul bar bya// de bzhin du ni slob dpon la// skal ba nyis 'gyur dbul bar bya// de nas grub pa gzhan rnams dang // rang gi/ 
14b4(rgyud): slob mar skal ba bzhin// de nas byin rlabs sbyor ba yis// phyag rgya dang ni lhan cig tu// rdo rje sems dpa'i ting 'dzin gyis// zas kyis sa bon dang ni bza'// skad cig de
14b5(rgyud): la gzugs brjes te// rdo rje sems dpa' lta bur gyur// gang dang gang gi gzugs rnams// sgrub par 'dodapa'i sngags pa yis// de dang de yi bsam gtan gyis// 
14b6(rgyud): blo gros brtan pas bza' bar bya// de dang de yi gzugasu ni// gdon mi za bar brje bar 'gyur// gzhan pa yi ni rdzas dag kyang // 'di nyid kyis ni bsgrub par bya// mig sman gyis ni mig
14b7(rgyud): byugs pas// khor yug tu ni mi snang 'gro/ snying la ldong ros kyis byugs na// yid kyi spyod yul nyid du 'gro/ ba bla yis ni lus byugs na// mkha' la nye bar 'gro bar 'gyur// mi sman
14b8(rgyud): nag po blangs nas su// nag po'i phyogs la bza' bar bya// de yi bshang ba'i mar khu las// dud pa mkhas pas bsgrub par bya// de yis mig la byugs nas ni// sangs rgyas kyis kyang mi
15a1(rgyud): gzigs shing // stobs ni dpal ldan rdo rje'i mtshon// nyid 'gyur rga dang 'chi ba med// mig smad dang ni ba lang mar// ma he dang nir nyid dang // mi yi mig sman nyid
15a2(rgyud): dag ni// mkhas pa yis ni blangs nas su// sngags pas gzung ste btso bar bya// mig sman chen po mchog tu bzang // 'di yis mig la byugs na ni// grub pa yid du 'ong bar 'gyur// mi
15a3(rgyud): snang 'grub pa thams cad kyis// blo gros chen po rgyal por 'gyur// sangs rgyas kun gyi sa chen po// nges par thob 'gyur gzhan du min// rdzas kyi gnas skabs le'u 'di// mtshungs med chen
15a4(rgyud): por nyer bshad do// gos dang gdug sogs ral gri dang / mtshon cha dam pa bsgrub par bya// snying po snying kar byas nas ni// bsgoms na myur du 'grub par 'gyur// rdo rje sems
15a5(rgyud): dpa' rgyal po ches// pad+ma'i sems dpa' bzhin ras mchog/ de yi zhal du byas nas su// de dang ldan pas bsgo/ ma par bya// mnga' bdag gang gis dbang phyug ltar// skad
15a6(rgyud): cig de la de 'gyur ro// de nyid kyi ni spyi bo'i char// mchog gi dam pa bsam gtan bya// skad cig de la mchod pa che'i// sangs rgyas su ni de 'gyuraro// de yi spyi gtsug nyid du ni// sna tshogs rdo rje
15a7(rgyud): bsgom par bya// de ni kun gyi rgyal dbang po// las kun byed pa'i don grub 'gyur// rdo rje snying kar bsam par bya// de yis dbus su snying po blta// de nas rdo rje rig pa 'dzin// mnga' bdag
15a8(rgyud): rdo rje'i dbang po 'grub// rin chen chen po che brgyad pa// snying ka ru ni mkhas pas sgom// der ni snying po bsam pa yis// rin chen rig pa 'dzin par 'gyur// pad+ma chen po 'dab brgyad pa/ 
15b1(rgyud): yid la bsgoms pas skad cig la// pad+ma che ldan mnga' bdag gis// pad+ma'i rig pa 'dzin par 'gyur// de la sogs pa mtha' yas pa// ji lta'i sbyor ba'i cho ga yis// mchog dang dman
15b2(rgyud): pa 'bring po yi// dngos grub dam pa bsgrub par bya// snying kar zla ba'i dkyil 'khor bsam// yi ge dam pa bsgom par bya// ji lta'i sbyor ba'i dkyil 'khor gyis// thams cad bdag tu bsgom
15b3(rgyud): par bya// de las langs te bdag zhi bas// zla 'od kha ba ltar bsil ba'i// 'od zer sprin gyis cher gtams pas// bsgrub bya'i spyi bor bzhag par bya// skad cig de la bdugs pa dang // gza'
15b4(rgyud): dang dug sogs rab 'phrogs shing // nyi ma gcig gam bdun nam ni// bsgrub bya zhi 'gyur gzhan du min// rin chen dkyil 'khor dbus gnas par// snying po'i mchog ni
15b5(rgyud): bsgom par bya// 'od zer ser po'i phreng mdzes pa// bsgomasapas de ni rgyas par byed// pad+ma'i dkyil 'khor dbus gnas par// mnyam par bzhag pas lha mo bsam// 
15b6(rgyud): dmar po'i rang bzhin 'bar dag pa// bsgrub bya'i sems la 'phro bar bya// slar yang bsdud pa'i sbyor ba yis// rang gi lus la gzhug par bya// 'khor los bsgyur ba lta bu yang // de ni ci
15b7(rgyud): nas dbang du 'gro/ las kyi dkyil 'khor dbus gnas par// sna tshogs rdo rje bsgom par bya// de yi dbus su yi ge ni// mar gad 'od 'dra bsgom par bya// 'od zer sprin gyis yang dag 'khrugs
15b8(rgyud): mkhas pa yis ni snying kar bsam// bsgrub bya la ni snying po'i 'od// bstims pa'i skad cig de la 'bab// rdo rje gar gyi gar byed cing // phyag rgya sbyor ba'i rnal 'byor dang // rdo rje rnal 'byor ma sbyor
15'a1(rgyud): pa'i / phyag rgyas thams cad ston par 'gyur// 'das pa dang ma 'ongs ci 'dod pa// lce brkyang bas ni smras par byed// 'dod dang mi 'dod dge mi dge/ rdo rje'i ngag gis
15'a2(rgyud): smra bar 'gyur// yang na legs par sbyar ba 'am// grong gi 'am tha mal skad dag gis// 'dod dang mi 'dod dge mi dge/ 'tshe ba 'am ni 'chi ba dang // nyams dang mi nyams rang gzhan gyi// de
15'a3(rgyud): dag thams cad de yis smras// de las gzhan du de mi smra// 'di ni bcom ldan rdo rje can// dbang bdag rdo rje'i dbyangs kyis gsungs// khros te lce rtser bsgoms nas su// lha mo yi ni snying po
15'a4(rgyud): mchog/ lcags kyu'i rnam par spros nas su// phyag rgya dang / ni phyag rgya'i lan// rlung la gzhag ste skad cig la/ da khrag rnams thams cad dgug par bya// char rgyun 'bab pa'i
15'a5(rgyud): sbyor ba yis// rang gi kha ru dbab par bya// de ni 'thungs bas sngags shes te// mnga' bdag rdo rje 'dzin pa'agyur// nam mkha' kun tu spyod dpal ldan// nyi ma'i snang
15'a6(rgyud): ba lta bur 'gyur// 'di nyid kyi ni rnal 'byor gyis// 'o ma zho dang mar bzang po// mar khu chu dang me tog kun// rlung gis dgu pa nyid du bya// zhags pas mgrin pa bcing byas te// lcags
15'a7(rgyud): kyu yis ni snying ka nas// rlung gis kun nas bteg nas su// lha mo de bzhin gnod sbyin mo// mi mo de bzhin lha min mo// brgyad brgya kho na bzlas pa yis// bud med tshul du dgug par bya// 
15'a8(rgyud): bsgrub bya sgrub byed ming spel nas// ka brtsig pa de bzhin khyim// dril bu rnams dang bum rnams la'ang // lha mo yi ni snying po yi// brgya bzlas pas ni 'bebs par 'gyur// shes
15'b1(rgyud): rab pa la byin ma mchog/ khro ba dang na yang dag ldan// gsal byed kyis ni gsal byas pas// las rnams dgan thams cad bya// du badzad namanyams pa/ 
15'b2(rgyud): mang ngo'i brgyad la bsdus nas su// byang du phyogs te bzhag par bya// de yi khar ni mnyam gzhag pas// gsang sngags legs par bzlas nas su// rdzas
15'b3(rgyud): dam pa ci rigs pa/ ba bla mig sman rdo tshwa dang / lding ros dang yang yang na btsag/ dkar rtsi sol ba nyid dang ni// gur gum dang ni rgya spos sam/ 
15'b4(rgyud): ru rta shu dag ga pur dang // tsan dan de bzhin a gu ru// sha dang khrag dang nyid dang ni// de bzhin sor mo'i gdu bu ni// rnal 'byor ldan pas bzhag nas kyang / 
15'b5(rgyud): de yi steng du bsdad la bkra// nyi ma shar nas de blangs/ bas// grub pa'i rig pa 'dzin par 'gyur/ dman pas dngos grub dman pa ste// rab kyis
15'b6(rgyud): rab tu rnam par bstan// bar mas bar mar shes par bya// mtshan ma med na dbang du byed ces so// skyes bu dag ni thams cad dang // bud med dag ni thams cad la/ 
15'b7(rgyud): reg pa tsam gyis dbang byed cing // mig la byugs pa yis kyang ngo // tsan dan gyis ni yongs byugs te// gur gum gyis ni thig le'o// la gu yis ni 'dug par bya/ 
15'b8(rgyud): dkar rtsi sol ba bcag gis ni// ji ltar 'dod pa'i ming dang ni// yongs su spel te ma bris pas// dbang ma song ba dbang 'gro ste/ rdo rje sems dpa'i
16a1(rgyud): / bka' bzhin no// khams kyis ming ni bris pa ni// dbang du byed pa'i mchog yin no// sol bas yongs su 'gugs par byed// dkar rtsi yis ni dug 'joms so// li khris skad cig/ 
16a2(rgyud): de nyid la// spro bar 'gyur bar the tsom med// ru rta a ga rus bdug pas// dbang du byed pa'i mchog yin no// sol bas yongs su 'gugs par byed// gnod sbyin mo ni nges par 'gugs// sha dang khrag gi bdug
16a3(rgyud): pa yi/ srin po 'gugs par byed pa'i mchog/ tsan+dan sil ha'i bdug pa yis// lha ni 'gugs par byed pa'i mchog/ ga bur tsan+dan 'dug pa yis// sangs rgyas mchog tu spyan 'dren pa'o// ga bur gang
16a4(rgyud): gis zos pa yis// gzhan du'ang de yi dbang du 'gyur// rig pa chen mo yi ge bzhi// mnyam par gzhag pa'i sbyor ba yis// 'khrugs pa dang ni spel ba'i dus/ nges par shib bsgrub par
16a5(rgyud): byad/ brtul zhugs can gyis gang bsgo ba'i// bka' lung de yis/ myur du byed// phrag par khur de bran po des// lhun po'i steng / du skyel bar 'gyur// grub pa yi ni mchog rab kyi// rdzas ni blangs nas/ 
16a6(rgyud): 'ongs par 'gyur// gtum po'i yi dgas nyi ma yi// rgyal gyi mtshan me sol ba bzung // gtum mo'i me tog khu ba yis// brtul zhugs bzang pos brtags nas su// pad+ma'i nang du gzhag par bya// de nyid mtshan mo
16a7(rgyud): gcig gam gsum// de las blangs te sbyor ba yis// mkhas pa yis ni mar zhu bya// de nas lha 'am grub pa 'am// sangs rgyas kyis kyang bsngags pa 'am// rigs sngags grub pa'i grib ma 'am// gdon mi za bar
16a8(rgyud): mthong bar 'gyur// 'gro dang mi 'gro'i skye bo rnams// dbang ma grub pa'ang dbang du byed// rang gi khrag gi ming bris la// de nyid kyis ni phye mas dgang // ji srid bskams par ma gyur par// de srid mi de 'ong bar
16b1(rgyud): 'gyur ba gang dang gang gis lha dag gis// rim pa 'di yis ming bris te// khro bo ldan pas bzlas par bya// de 'di skad cig de la 'grub// de yi bka' bzhin byed pa dang // ngang gis de ni dbang du 'gyur// dkon
16b2(rgyud): mchog gsum la gnod byed pa// bsad pa'i don du sngags rig pas// 'bar ba'i phreng ba 'khrugs pa'i 'od// zhal bzhi pa la tshar 'jigs pa// zhags pa lcags kyu thod pa can// bdag nyid myur du bsam
16b3(rgyud): par bya// gsang sngags dang spel ba yis// ming ni sol bas bris nas su// gdug pa de ni mnan nas kyang // rang gi gdug pa'i sems kyis bsnun// 'di nyid kyi ni ting 'dzin gyis// nges pa ru yang nges par
16b4(rgyud): byed da khams kyi sa bon dang spel ba'i// khams kyi ming ni bris nas su// khams de yang dag mnan nas ni// khang pa ru ni rgyun tu bzhag/ de ni myur du nges 'gyur te/ de srid du ni mi g.yor
16b5(rgyud): gnas// rma bya'i sgro 'am gtsug phud kyis// yongs su blangs la/ bsgrub par bya// rma bya zhes bya'i rtsa ba yi// mkhas pa yis ni/ yongs su bzung // dmag la sngags rig pas bskor bas// de nas
16b6(rgyud): dmag dpung 'jig pa dang // rmongs pa'am ni rengs pa 'am// skad cig de la 'khor bar 'gyur/ khyi dang pag dang bya rog gi/ mig ni yongs su blangs nas su// mig sman dang ni mnyam por bya// lha mo'i sngags kyis
16b7(rgyud): bsngags pa yis// sgrub pa po yi gzugs rnams kun// 'jigs par 'gyur bar the tsom med/ tsiN+Di'i me tog btsud nyid kyis// lcags kyi g.yogs pa'i sbyor ba yis// de yi kha ru nges bcug pas// rga shi med
16b8(rgyud): par rnam par rgyu// rims gtong gzugs ni legs bris te// de yi kha ru gnod byed ni// sbyor ba yis ni bcug nas su// yongasu mnan la shin tu bzlas// rims gtong de yi gzugs kyis ni// rab tu 'dzin par
17a1(rgyud): / gdon mi za// gza' 'am yang dag yi dgas sam// gnod sbyin dang ni srin po dang // gzhan pa yi ni nad rnams kyis// 'dzin pa la ni dpyad mi dgos// gshin rje bris te bskrad par bya// de yi/ 
17a2(rgyud): zhal du dgra bo ste// rmongs pa'i bdag nyid mi 'gro na// de ni myur du nges par 'chi// bsad pa la yang 'di nyid kyis// yongasu mnan nas nges par bzlo// gang du gter ni yod snyam gyur// der ni sngags rig pa/ 
17a3(rgyud): song ste/ lce yongs bzung la bzlas pa bya// de yis gsal po'i tshig gis smra// tshad dang yod dang med pa dang // dgegs dang bgegs ni ji ltar gnas// ji srid de ni dgyes smras na// de la gtor ma sbyin
17a4(rgyud): par bya// gal te bgegs ni mi sman// der ni mchod yon rab tu brtag/ dbus mo gnyis btsugs gus pa yis// no 'dzin sangs rgyas yum las so// phyogs bzhi dag tu phur bus
17a5(rgyud): gang po// de nas gnas rnams bskrad par bya// de nas mtshams ni bcing bar bya// mnyam par bzhag ste bskor bar bya/ sbyor ba shes pas sngags 'di yis// de nas rdzas ni gdon par
17a6(rgyud): bya// oM ba su de sar+b+ba ar+tha sA d+ha ni sA d+ha ya sA d+hA ya u d+ha ra u d+ha rak+Sha rAk+Sha/ sarbAr+tha ni tsa ye ta ta tsa tsaT Ta ha ha swA hA// yang na rig po 'di yis kyang // las rnams dag ni thams cad bya// phyogs bcing ba

17b1(rgyud): skal ba bzang po gnyis dbul lo// gzhan pa yi ni spyan rnams la// rdo rje theg pa rtogs gyur pa'i// skal ba re ni sbyin par bya// gzhan du dam tshig gdung bar 'gyur// 'di ni bcom ldan rnal 'byor can//

17b3(rgyud): cig dpa' bo che// yum rnams kun gyi dkyil 'khor nino// rgyal po'i dbang phyug rab gsol ba// sems can thams cad 'dir 'thung ba'o// de nas bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi
17b4(rgyud): bdag po'i dbang phyug dpal zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la mnyam par bzhag nas nyid kyi sku dang gsung dang thugs nga rdo rje las phyung ngo // dkyil 'khor ji ltar sngar gsungs pa// 'on
17b5(rgyud): kyang seng ge'i khri dang ldan// de yi steng du pad+ma che// der ni ri bong can dkyil 'khor// de yi steng du nyi ma che// nyi ma der ni dkyil 'khor mchog/ cha brgyad pa la dbus rin chen// de yi ste
17b6(rgyud): du rgyal po'i yum// ser dang sngo ba'i 'od chen po// gser gyi ngo bo dang tshungs pa// phyag gnyis kyis ni chos 'chad cing // g.yas pa yi ni mchog sbyin pa// g.yon gyi rin chen lan bu mchod// rgyan
17b7(rgyud): rnams kun gyis rnam par brgyan// gos ni 'phyang zhing sna tshogs pa// gtsug tor mu tog thor tshugs can// de yi mdun du rin chen bri// g.yon du bum pa bzang po mchog/ g.yas pa ru ni dpag bsam shing /

18a1(rgyud): babacu drug phyi rol tu/ ser po'i gos kyis yongs su dkris// me tog ser po sogs kyis brgyan/ de mdun blo ldan pa bya ba/ sbyin pa'i pha rol phyin dge ma/ dmar dang ser dang ches dkar
18a2(rgyud): ba rin chen ldan pa'i phag sbyin pa// ser po'i 'od ldan phreng mdzes ma// rin chen bzang po kun gyis sras// mkha' yi nyi zla skar ma yis// kun nas yongs su bskor ba'o// gtsug pud cod pan gos la sog/ 
18a3(rgyud): / phreng ba dang ldan dgas pa mo// de yi lho ru bri bya ba// tshul khrims pha rol phyin dge ma// cung zad ser ba'i rin chen lus// sna tshogs rgyan gyis rnam par brgyan// sna tshogs gos ni yongasu gyon// mdzes pa'i phreng
18a4(rgyud): ba'i chun po'i gtsug/ gos ldan gtsug na gtsug tor mchog/ yid bzhin rin chen dam pa'i phyag// g.yon pa'i skyil krungs da rin chen bzang // cho ga ji bzhin rab tu bsam// rgyab tu bzod pa
18a5(rgyud): ma zhes bya// cung zad 'dzum zhing ser mdzes ma// dmar po'i gos ni legs par gyon// rin po che yi rgyan gyis brgyan// thams cad rin chen mchog 'dri zhing // dmar po'i gos ni 'byung ba ma/

18a7(rgyud): yang ku la sngo bsang dkar// rdo rje seng ge'i khri la bzhugs// lhag ma rnams ni zhag bya ba// dkyil 'khor byas te rin chen ldan// sgo dang sgo ru sgo ba ma// rin chen kun gyis rnam par brgyan// de nas phyi yi phyi
18a8(rgyud): nyid du// rin chen snyim pa'i lag pa mchog/ phyogs skyong ba ni thams cad ni// go rims bzhin du bzhag par bya// de yi phyi rol thams cad du// mkhas pas klu dang gnod sbyin bri// rin chen bum pa bzang po dang
18b1(rgyud): gdugs dang rgyal mtshan ba dan lag/ gtor ma rnam pa sna tshogs dang // lha ba shos rab tu bzang dge ba// bzang dang btung ba'i ro mchog dang // mer dang ke ra nyid dang ni// zho dang bu ram hwags dang bcas// 'o/ 
18b2(rgyud): ma mar dang sbrang rtsi dang // rgyal po bza' ba dam pa'i mchog/ bza' ba la sogs rab mchog go// de nas sngags pas 'jug par bya// rgyan rnams kun gyis brgyan nas su// ser po'i gos 'dzin dag pa
18b3(rgyud): dang / phreng ldan dri zhim ldan pa'i las// sgo yi char ni zhugs na su// thog mar lha ni spyan drang bya// phyag rgya bcings te dbyangs snyan nas// rab tu dga' ba'i yid kyis su// lhar bcas 'jig rten dag
18b4(rgyud): la sman slad du// kun tu bzang po'i smon lam dran mdzod la// rin chen dam pa seng ge'i khrir bzhugs te// 'khor bo cas lha dang de bzhin gshegs pa spyon// de nas de dag legs byon te// 
18b5(rgyud): sras bcas 'khor dang bcas rnams kyang // sems can rnam/ la dngos grub ster// sgrub pa po la khyad par du// de nas thal mo legs sbyar la// rin chen gyis bkang me tog bcas// 
18b6(rgyud): gsang sngags brjod de gtor bar bya// ci bde bar ni bzhe su gsol// de nas rang gi dbang bskur bya// de yi sngags dang phyag rgya yis// sa la lag pas reg nas su// bsnyems pa yis ni mthon par bya// 
18b7(rgyud): de nas slob ma gzhug par bya// me tog dris ni yang dag sdud// ser po'i gos bzang yang dag gyon// lag na drin chen dri bzang po// dga' dang bcas te snyim pa de// snga ma'i sngags kyis dor bar bya// gang gi
18b8(rgyud): drung du lhung gyur pa// lha de de yi 'grub pa yin// de nas g.yas nas rnam bskor te// slob ma de ni 'byung bar bya// bzang po'i seng ge'i khrir bzhag ste// dbang bskur ba yi sbyor ba byas// gdugs dang rgyal mtshan
19a1(rgyud): / ba dan dang // mdzes pa'i rnga yab g.yob pa yis// de bzhin du yang dbang bskur te// bum pa brgyad dang bcu drug la// de yi sngags dang phyag rgya yis// go rims ji lta ba bzhin no// de nas sbyor ba de
19a2(rgyud): 'ongs te// 'khor los bsgyur ba'i rim pa yis// 'khor lo rin chen bzang po'i lag/ rgyal ba rgyal ba'i sgra dge bas// gsang ba'i sbyor ba'i rnal 'byor gyis// lte ba ru ni dbang bskur ro// 'di bdag
19a3(rgyud): gtor can rin chen 'dzin// rdo rje rin chen 'dzin par 'gyur// dam tshig gi ni dam pa yis// sangs rgyas kun gyi don rgyas pa// 'bad pas de ring blangs pa yis// phongs pa'i dri ma 'phrog par byed// de nas
19a4(rgyud): dpa' bo 'chi med 'dzin// rin chen tshogs kyis mchod par bya// gzhan pa yi yang du ma ni// rgyal po dbang phyug dam pa ngas so// de bzhin dbang bskur lnga po yis// skabs med kyang ni
19a5(rgyud): bdag med 'gyur// gling bzhi dbang phyug dpal ldan yang // gnod pa med par thob par 'gyur// gsang ba las kyang ches shin tu// gsang ba yi ni mna' bsgrags te// de yi sgom
19a6(rgyud): dang sgrub pa'i thabs// slob ma la ni de nas bslab// gur gum dang ni tsan+dan dang // dri dang mar me bzang po la// dam tshig gi ni gsal byas pa// lan gsum du ni 'thung du gzhug/ bu kye 'thung shig gsang
19a7(rgyud): pab cheHdam tshig tu ni 'da' ba dka'// gal te 'di las 'das gyur na// myur ba nyid du 'chi bar 'gyur// shi nas kyang ni dmyal sdug bsngal// rab mang du 'bod nyid du gnas// gal te mi rung skye 'dod pa
19a8(rgyud): 'am// nam zhig dngos grub thob 'dod na// de bzhin 'phongs pa'i sdug bsngal las// ring du nges par khyod kyis skyobs// 'di dag legs thos slob ma la// gsang ba'i sgrub thabs bshad par bya// 
19b1(rgyud): ltar rgyal rigs bum mi// bzung nas gsal pa'i rnal 'byor bya// nyi ma bdun na nges par 'grub// rgyal po'i phun tshogs thob par gyur/ shes rab rol phyin pa'i mchog dkyil 'khor sbyor bas bsam/ 
19b2(rgyud): gtan bya// rgyal mo cho ga bzhin bzung ste// sgrub pa pos ni myur du 'grub// nyi ma gsum gyi rgyal po mchog/ gdon mi za bar thob par 'gyur// bram ze'i bu mo skal chen mo// nor chen la ni bsgrub par bya// rje rigs
19b3(rgyud): sna tshogs sbyor ba yis// mtshungs pa nyid du bsgrub par bya// de yis dngos grub mchog rnyed de// rgyal po 'jig rten gsum gyi rjed// dmangs mo dpa' bo'i sbyor ba yis// bsgrubs na sngags kyi dngos grub
19b4(rgyud): 'gyur te/ gnod sbyin rgyal mchog grub pa dang // gnod sbyin rnam das kyi dbang phyug mchog/ dman pa'i sems su bshad/ pa dang // mchog gi mchog ni chen po dang // bar mas bar ma
19b5(rgyud): dngos grub ni// skye ba 'di la thob par 'gyur// de nas las rnam sa bslab par bya// zhi ba dang ni rgyas pa'i las// de bzhin dbang dang mngon spyod dang // gzhan pa yi yang sna tshogs ni// 
19b6(rgyud): sems can rnams la dga' ba'o// shes rab pha rol phyin dge ma// dkyil 'khor sbyor bas bsgom par bya// kun da dkar po zla ba 'dra// 'od zer dkar pos mdzes pa mo// skye bo nad pa 'chi ka ma// de yi lus la
19b7(rgyud): gzhug par bya// de nas de ni stobs ldan 'gyur// brgyad gnyis pa yi lang tsher ldan// nad rnams kun las rnam par grol// rga dang 'chi ba rnam par spangs// bstan bcos kun gyi don rig cing // shes rab
19b8(rgyud): dran pa mchog dang ldan// de bzhin rang 'gyur rnal 'byor pa// nam mkha' la ni yang dag sgom// mdzes pa'i rin chen sna tshogs pa'i// thams cad du ni char 'bab pa// 'di yis phongs pa rnam par sel// phongs
20a1(rgyud): pa rnams la rab tu brtag/ mthe bong yi ni tshad tsam pa'i// nor rgyun ma yi rnam pa bya// lha mo la ni mnyam par bzhag/ de yi mdun du gsang sngags bzlas// ji srid 'bum phrag kho na ste/ 
20a2(rgyud): de nas dngos grub bsgrub par bya// zla ba gang ba 'am bcu bzhi 'am// brgyad pa 'am gzas bzung nyin par la// mchod pa chen po byas nas su// mkhas pas mtshan mo thog thag bzlas// de nas dga' bas
20a3(rgyud): gzugs brnyan de// gdon mi za bar 'bar bar 'gyur// de nas bzung ste mdor bsdu na// mi yi 'khor los bsgyur bar 'gyur// bzlas pas mtshan ma bzang byung na// rnal 'byor pa ni nor chen 'gyur// bar mas
20a4(rgyud): gling ni thob par 'gyur// tha ma yis ni khor yug go// thams cad du ni bzlas tsam gyis// longs spyod zad par 'gyur ma yin// rgyal po thams cad dbang 'gyur zhing // bud med thams cad
20a5(rgyud): dga' bar 'gyur// snying kar rnal 'byor byas nas su// nor bu lag par bcangs nas ni// nyi ma'i dkyil 'khor la gnas sgom// myur du rin chen rgyal por 'gyur// phyag rgya 'di na byas
20a6(rgyud): gyur pas// rtag tu sgom pas bsgom par bya// ji ltar 'dod pa'i grub rnyed de// rdo rje 'dzin pa ji bzhin no// zhes bcom ldan 'das rdo rje sems dpas bka' stsal to// de nas sbyor ba ji bzhin du// yum de rnams ni
20a7(rgyud): legs byon nas// las kyi dkyil 'khor legs gnas pa// ston pa la ni zhu ba zhus// gang du rgyal ba kun bzhugs nas// bla na med pa'i don mdzad pa// sems can kun la bde slad du// myur du las ni 'grub
20a8(rgyud): pa lag so// de nas bcom ldan 'das las thams cad kyi dam pa'i dpal zhes bya ba'i ting 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs nas// de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi yum gyi dam tshig dam pa de rnams la las kyi/ 
20b1(rgyud): dkyil 'khor bka' stsal pa/ rlung gi dkyil 'khor bri bar bya// de yi dbus su gru gsum pa// de yi steng du lha mo bzhag/ 'bar ba'i me dang mtshungs pa la// zhal bzhi ma la cher 'jigs pa// mche ba rab tu
20b2(rgyud): gtsigs pa mo// thod pa'i phreng ba'i cod pan can// rdo rje lcags kyu thod pa dang // zhags pa g.yas dang g.yon par 'dzin// lpags pa chen pogs su gyon// khro mo mig 'bras rab byung ba// mtshabs mchu mnan
20b3(rgyud): zhal chen mo// de yi mdun du bri bya ba// mtha' ma'i zhal ni mdor sdus pa// sna tshogs gtum dang drag pa'i zhal// du ma'i phyag gis yang dag 'khrugs// zhags pa lcags kyu thod sogs dang // rdo rje can gyi sog
20b4(rgyud): le 'dzin// thod pas lus la bres gyur cing // cod pan chen pos 'jigs byed mo// gshen rje dpa' bos bri bya ba// mtha' gdong dam pa yi ni mchog/ sngon po 'bar ba'i rang bzhin khros// 
20b5(rgyud): mgo bo'i phreng bas rnam par brgyan// thod pa'i phreng ba'i cod pan/ can// stag gi lpags pa'i sham thabs can// rel gri rin chen thod pa dang // rin chen dbyug gu 'dzin pa'i mchog/ de nas
20b6(rgyud): lha mo legs bri ba// pad+ma'i zhal ma 'jigs chen po// dmar mo phyag na nyi zla 'dzin// bskal pa'i me dang mtshungs pa mo// g.yon pa ru ni khro mo che// ma spyom ma ni ska rags mgul// las kyi rdo rje dri ldan mchog/ 
20b7(rgyud): mche ba rnam par gtsigs pa'i zhal// gtsug na thod pa 'jigs su rung // rab gtum stobs dang gsal ba mo// 'byor ldan cho ga rig pas bris// phyi rol tu ni legs bri ba// khro bcas 'jigs pa dang bcas pa/ 
20b8(rgyud): ral pa'i thor tshugs chen po can// khrag gis gang ba'i thod pa dang // phyag rgya bzang pos phyag mtshan pa'o// de yaM byi ru lha rnams ni// snying pa rab sbyar yi dam pa// thams cad du ni yongs su bzhag
21a1(rgyud): 'jig rten skyong ba bzhag par bya// sgo rnams dag ni thams cad du// sgra stong ba yang de bzhin du// de nas gtor ma'i cho ga ni// sha bcas btang ba ro dang ldan// de nas go cha bcings gyur pa/ 
21a2(rgyud): thod pa'i cod pan chen po dang // khrag gam chang gis bkang ba 'am// thod pa ldan pas 'jug par bya// thams cad 'grub pa'i ma mo rnams// 'di yis spyan ni drang bar bya// dkon mchog gsum la
21a3(rgyud): gnod byed pa'i// gsang ba'i don du ma mo rnams// de ring nyid du dkyil 'khor 'dir// 'jigs chen ma rnams thams cad gshegs// 'jigs pa'i sgra dang che rag tu ma dang // kha nas 'od zer stong
21a4(rgyud): phrag ni// mthong ba dang ni thos pa na// mtshan mar yang ni shes par bya// de nas de yis a rag sbyin// ci bder bzhes da cig 'jigs mdzad ma// gdug pa chen po gsol bar mdzod// 
21a5(rgyud): gdug gtum 'jigs par byed pa yis// de nas bdag la dbang bskur te// thod par gnas pa'i ro yis ni// srang tsam rgya ni sha zos nas// ma mo thams cad bsgrub par bya// de nas mngon
21a6(rgyud): spyod las rnams kun// dam tshig bsrung ba yis ni bya// dkon mchog gsum la gnod byed dang // bla ma rnams la 'khyal smra ba// rtag tu gsod par lha mo rnams// bgyid par bdag ni rjes su bzung // 
21a7(rgyud): de nas cho ga de nyid kyis// slob ma'i dam pa gzhug par bya// khro bo'i lha la bskul nas su// me tog dmar po dor bar bya// bdag gi me tog dam pa 'di// ci bde bar ni bzhes su gsol// bdug pa 'di ni
21a8(rgyud): bzung nas su// gsol byed 'di ni gsol bar mdzod// lha mo gang la ltung gyur pa// de yis de la mchog gsil lo// de nas dbang bskur byin nas su// dkyil 'khor gyi ni mdun bzhag ste// thong
21b1(rgyud): par ru ni gnas pa yis// khrag gis dbang ni bskur bar bya// de nas sgo ru bos nas su// dam tshig 'bad pas 'dzin du gzhug/ rab tu gdug pa'i snying gi khrag/ bzang po 'di ni 'thung zhig bu// zong shig/ 
21b2(rgyud): zo shig sha chen po// btung ba 'jigs pa chen po 'thung // gzhan du na ni 'chi 'gyur te// mkha' 'gro ma dang gza' rnams dang // gnod sbyin srin po gtum po yi// ring por mi thogs rab tu za/ 
21b3(rgyud): de nas mngon spyod las rnams ni// stong phrag dag ni bslab par bya// de yi sbyor ba'i rnal 'byor gyis// rang nyid khro bor bzung gyur nas// gnod byed thams cad bsad par bya// dgra rnams thams cad
21b4(rgyud): bza' bar bya// gdug pa thams cad bca' bar bya// srin po thams cad gzhom par bya// mtha' yas zhal// ma'i sbyor ba yis// bsad dang bzung ba de yis bya// zhal ba ni
21b5(rgyud): ma yis sbyor ba yis// thams cad 'gugs pa'i dam pa yin// mkha' gdong ma yis thams cad du// rin po che yi cho ga sa 'byung ngo // pad+ma'i zhal gyi sbyor ba yis// chang gi dam pa
21b6(rgyud): btung bar bya// ma spyom ma yi sbyor ba yis// sha ni 'gugs pa'i mchog yin no// nam mkha' rengs pa chen po ste// dmag dpung 'byor pa'i dam pa'o// rmugs dang rmongs pa thams cad du// 
21b7(rgyud): dpyad pa ru ni mi bya'o// sngar bshad pa yi las rnams dang // ma bshad pa la ci 'dod pa// bzlas pa tsam gyis kun bya ste// thams cad du ni the tsom med// dur khrod kyi ni thal ba la// dgra bo
21b8(rgyud): gzugs ni 'bad pas bye// ming dang spel bar byas nas su// ma mo'i ral gris btub par bya// de nas nyi ma bdun na ni// brlab par 'gyur bar gdon mi za// gang lus ji ltar bcad gyur pa// 
22a1(rgyud): de dang de yi yan lag 'chad// zhal bzhi ma yi sbyor ba yis// sngags pa mnyam par bzhag pas bcad// de yi mgrin par zhags pa ni// mkhas pas spros te bcing bar bya// 
22a2(rgyud): lcags kyus snying khar phug nas su// rlung gis bskyod de drang bar bya// de nas de yi ming bskul nas// de ni shes rab ldan pas dgug/ dman dang mchog gi dbye ba yis// 'di yis 'bras
22a3(rgyud): bung yis bshad// mdor bsdus pas ni shes par bya// sngags pa'i rgyal po'i sbyor ba yis shes so// de nas bcom ldan 'das ma de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad ni// de yis dngos
22a4(rgyud): grub gsol mi 'gyur// nye bar 'tshe ba 'jigs rnams da dang // gdon dang gnod sbyin srin po bcas// mi zadand kyis btab nas su// shi nas mnar med nyid du 'gyur// 
22a5(rgyud): de nas de bzhin dbang bskur gyis// dkyil 'khor la bzhag yum rnams kyis// dbang bskur gsang ba'i dam tshig sbyin// gsang ba'i sgrub thabs nyan du gzhug/ rang yum ma
22a6(rgyud): mo'i sa bon gyis// rang gi rnam rtog bdag yum min// lta bus yab gyur bsgrubs na ni// nyi ma bdun na rab tu 'grub// sangs rgyas kun gyi yab ston pa// kun mkhyen ye shes spyod yul
22a7(rgyud): te/ drag po kun dang bde chen po// ye shes kun gyi mchog gi mchog/ shes rab kyis ni thams cad sgrub// las rgyas pa yi dam pa'i mchog/ bye brag tu ni bskul nas su// byang chub kyi ni
22a8(rgyud): yon+dan gyi// thams cad du ni 'od gsal ba'i// dngos grub thams cad bsgrub par bya// shes rab kyi ni las dbye bas// gzugs dang dbyibs nyid dag gis so// phyag rgya dang ni phyag rgya'i lan// 
22b1(rgyud): de bzhin dkyil 'khor dam tshig dang // bzas dang ni nyer spyod pa// gtor ma lha bshos nyid dang ni// shin tu bde ba'i stan nyid dang // de dang de ni nges par sbyar// bzlas dang bsam gtan sa bon ni// 
22b2(rgyud): rang gi lus khyab pa nyid do// gsang sngags dag ni thams cad las// gsang sngags 'di ni rab tu sngags// tshe 'dir dam pa'i rjes grub cing // gdon mi za bar thob par 'gyur// 'di ni bcom
22b3(rgyud): ldan kun rdo rje// ye shes 'byung gnas mnga' bdag gsungs// las kun gyi ni sbyor ba yis// 'di ni sgyu mes 'gro la bzhugs// de nas de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi yum de rnams
22b4(rgyud): kyis bcom ldan 'das la 'di skad ces gsol to// phyag rgya'i ye shes mchog tu dge/ ye shes chen pos gsung du gsol// gang gis mngon par rgyas btab
22b5(rgyud): kun// mnga' bdag dus mi ring bar 'grub// de nas bcom ldan 'das kyis yang ting nge 'dzin rdo rje zhes bya ba'i ting / nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs nas 'di skad ces bka' stsal
22b6(rgyud): to// phyag rgya rtags su yang dag bshad// tha snyad tsam du rnam par brtags// sangs rgyas kun gyi kla klo'i skad// phyag rgya thams cad yang dag bshad// 'on kyang mgon po mchog gi
22b7(rgyud): brtags// lag pa'i rnam dgod mtshan ma nyid// gang gi yid ches legs skye rnams// dam tshig shes pa'i lha rnams ni// sgrub po rnams kyis rab bskul na// grub pa'i dam pa rab tu stsol// 
22b8(rgyud): dus las thams cad byon nas su// slar yang gshegs pa nyid du 'gyur// lag pa zla ba nyi mar bya// shes rab thab su rab tu brtag/ de nas sngags pas yongasu sbyar// rang gi sa bon dag gis mtshan
23a1(rgyud): oM pra dz+nyo pA ya sa mA yog/ de nas thal mo nges par sbyar// phan tshun rjes su rtogs chen po// khu tshur shin tu bzhag par bya// khu tshur bsdams pa lta bur bcing // so so run
23a2(rgyud): sbyor bar bya// snying gi dbus su nges par bzung // g.yon pa'i steng du log pa g.yas// bzhag ste sor mo so sor bya// lag g.yas sgreng nas phyogs kun tu// 'khor lo'i sbyor bas spro bar bya/ 
23a3(rgyud): rdo rje sgo lcogs lta bur bskum// sor mo thams cad rtsibs su bya// oM sa d+harma tsakra sa ma ye// de bzhin g.yon pas yongs su spro// so ri mo rtsibs kyi sbyor ba yis// shes rab steng du bsgreng bar bya// gomam
23a4(rgyud): pa yang ni de bzhin no// rtse mo cung zad sbyar bar bya// chos kyi las ni chen po byed// de nyid snyam du bskums pa ni// las kyi phyag rgya zhes su grags// de bzhin ming med byas na su// lhag ma rnams ni gdod du sbyar/ 
23a5(rgyud): phyag rgya chen po shin tu ni// dngos grub thams cad rab tu gsol// phyag rgya 'di rnams bsdams na ni// rang nyid shes rab bdag/ por 'gyur// kun tu bzang po rgyal po che// lha dang lha min bcas/ 
23a6(rgyud): pas mchod ce'o// de nas ma mo de rnams kun// slar yang gtso bo le bstod nas// shes rab chen po rnam bzhi yi// phyag rgya zhu ba rnam par byas// phyag rgya bzhi yi rab kyi mchog/ bcom ldan 'das kyis
23a7(rgyud): bka' stsol cig/ gsang ba'i phyag rgya'i yal ga mchog/ shes rab thabs kyis lus bzang ba// gang zhig gsang ba'i rnal 'byor ni// gang gi rnal 'byor pa bde ba// rdzu 'phrul 'phel dang yang dag pa'i// 
23a8(rgyud): rdzu 'phrul skye ba 'dir rnyed pa// bcom ldan ston pas bka' stsal pa// gsang ba'i phyag rgya rgyal ba'i gzhi// gang gi myur du sgrub po kun// rab tu bde bar gnas pas 'grub// de nas bcom ldan rdo rje can/ 
23b1(rgyud): mnyes te gsang ba'i dam pa gsungs// phyag rgya'i pha rol phyin pa rnams// bde ba chen po rab tu sgrub// rdo rje thal mo dam par bsdams// rdo rje dbus su bzhag par bya// gsang ba'i dam tshig zhes su bsgrags// 
23b2(rgyud): gsang ba'i rnal 'byor rab tu sgrub// de nyid rdo rje lta bur byas// bskyod pas bde ba bskyed par byed// 'di ni chos 'dzin zhes bya ba'i// phyag rgya gsang ba sgrub pa'o// g.yon par thabs ni bskums nas su/ 
23b3(rgyud): bskyod pas bde ba 'gugs par byed// dag pa'i las zhes rab tu grags// bde ba thams cad rab stsol byed// de nyid kha dang rkan la ni// sbyar ba chen mo zhes su bshad// rdo rje phan tshun yang dag sbyar// lcags
23b4(rgyud): klu'i kha ni bskyod par bya// kha ni phan tshun yongs sbyar ba// gsang bra'i zhags pa zhes su grags// de bzhin bskums par byas nas su// dam du bsdams te bcing bar bya// 'di ni gsang ba sdems pa'i/ 
23b5(rgyud): rgya// ye shes sdems pa rab tu 'grub// thams cad rdo rje ltar rdo rje/ de bzhin bskyod cing bskor bar bya// de 'di gsang ba rab tshim pa// tshim pa'i don ni ster bar byed// lhag ma phyag rgya chen po ru/ 
23b6(rgyud): shes bya phyag rgya mdor bsdus pa'o// de nyid las kyis phyag rgya mchog/ las kyi dbye bas sbyar bar bya// zhes so// de nas ma mo de rnams kun// yid ni tshim zhing mgu ba yis// rdo rje sems dpa' mtshan yangs pa'i/ 
23b7(rgyud): legs so ba ni nges par phul// legs so legaso gsong chen po// legaso legaso mchod chen po// legaso leg so rnal 'byor che// legaso le gso rab tshim mdzad// de nas bcom ldan 'das ma rnams dang / 
23b8(rgyud): de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi rdo rje btsun mo rnams kyis dgyes pa'i dkyil 'khor zhu ba bcom ldan 'das la zhus pa// sangs rgyas rang bzhin khyod la 'dud// spyod pa'i rin chen khyod la 'dud// dam pa'i rgyu 'gyur
24a1(rgyud): khyod la 'dud// sna tshogs mdzad pa khyod la 'dud// dpa' bo 'dul ba khyod la 'dud// gsangs pa'i chos ldan khyod la 'dud// zhi ba'i thugs la phyag 'tshal 'dud// mgon po khyod
24a2(rgyud): la bdag cag zhu// bdag gi dkyil 'khor zhu ba'i phyir// mnga' bdag rgyal dang sems can rnams// de nas bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyis rdo rje btsun mo'i dkyil 'khor
24a3(rgyud): bka' stsal pa// de lta'i dkyil 'khor bris nas su// dbus su pha rol phyin ma dgod// d+hI zhes bya ba shes rab can// thabs dang ldan pas gsal byas pa// 'di yis sngags pa 'jigs med
24a4(rgyud): par// zla ba phyed kyis nges par 'gyur// rig pa 'di yis de yis ni// las rnams thams cad byed pa dang // dbang dang dgug dang dbye ba dang // tshim dang 'phrog dang 'bras chen po/ 
24a5(rgyud): zhibs zhi ba zhes su bshad// brnyes ma zhes pas rgyas par/ bshad// dbang dang dgug dang dbye ba la// byed ma'o dbang la drag mo yin// sha yi mtha' ru bdud gsod ma// gsod pa
24a6(rgyud): dang ni spel bar bya// 'gro ba dang ni yang dag ldan// sor mo zhags pas dkri bar bya// thams cad du ni drag po dgu/ drag po drag po'i go 'phang gnas// 'di yi cho ga ldan pa yis// las kyis tshogs kyi
24a7(rgyud): mchog kun bya// sems la rnal 'byor legs bsam te// brgyad brgya khon bzlas pa yis// dbang bcas nyid dam dbang chen po// stobs kyis mgo bo mnan nas su// mamo'i tshogs kun de yis
24a8(rgyud): bzla// dus mi ring bar 'grub par 'gyur// gzi brjid chen pos bka' bzhin du// mgo bos nye bar phyag 'tshal te// 'di yis ma mo thams cad kun// gzi brjid kyis ni gzi ldan pa// sngags kyi rgyal po
24b1(rgyud): 'od ldan pas// go rims ji lta ba bzhin du// dpe zla med pa'i dngos grub byed// grub pa'i lam la rab tu gnas// sangs rgyas rdo rje 'dzin pa yi// 'phrul dang rnam par 'phrul pa yi// 'di ni ston pa chen/ 
24b2(rgyud): bos gsungs// ma skyes skye ba med la bzhugs// rtag pa ston pa thams cad pa// namakha' nyi zla dri ma med// de dag thams cad rab dga' ste// dngos po spangs pa'i btsun me yis// gar dang glu dang sil
24b3(rgyud): snyan mchog/ bzhad dang sgeg pa'i sbyor ba dang // bud med sgyu ma'i rnam 'phrul dang // gling bu pi wang rdza rnga sogs// ting ting shag dang dung sgra dang // ro dang reg pa dri chen po// gzugs dang sgra sogs bde
24b4(rgyud): ldan pas// dpa' chen la ni mchod byas nas// snyems dang bica das pas phyag 'tshal te// slar yang mgon po la gsol btab// rdo rje btsun mo'i dkyil 'khor rnams// mgon po ci
24b5(rgyud): yi phyir mi gsungs// yab rnams kyi ni thams cad dang // yum rnams kyi ni mdor bsdus pa// mchod pa yang ni tham sa cad de// bran bcas po nya pho nya mo// 'jig rten pa ni mtha'
24b6(rgyud): dag gi/ gtso bo chen pos gsung du gsol// de nas bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi bdag pos yang de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad gnyi su med pa rnam par 'phrul pa zhes
24b7(rgyud): bya ba'i ting 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs nas// de dag nyid kyi sku dang gsung dang thugs rdo rje la gzhug pa dang / dgug pa dang / bcings pa dang / mnyes par bya ste/ nyid kyi sku dang gsung thugs rdo rje
24b8(rgyud): gnyi su med pa bsgyings pa dang / ldan pa la mnyam par gzhag ste bzhug so// de nas yang bde ba yongasu skyes pa rab tu dgyes pa'i sangs rgyas thams cad lhan cig spyod pa dang bcas pa/ bran dang
25a1(rgyud): bcas pas de la 'di skad ces gsol to// mgon pa dbang phyug du rje sems// rdo rje snang ba mdzes pa'i sra// gsang ba rgyan gyi dkyil 'khor na// dpa' bo chen pos gsung du gson
25a2(rgyud): gang gi rgyal ba kun skyed pa// byang chub sems dpa' grags chen po// de nas bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi gsang ba rgyan gyi bkod pa dkyil 'khor chen po'i mchog
25a3(rgyud): ces bya ba'i ting 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs nas 'di skad ces gsol to// e ma sangs rgyas thams cad kyis// zhu ba rab tu zhus pa ni// gang phyir nga la dngos med kyang // zhu ba zhus pa thams
25a4(rgyud): cad thos// gsang ba chen po'i smon lam dang // de bzhin snying rje'i pha rol phyin// dran pa med las dran pa yang // dran 'gyur dran po bzhin gnas pa// sangs rgyas kun gyi
25a5(rgyud): gsang chen po// shes rab pha rol phyin dge ba// chos dang chos min rnam par spangs// brjod du med pa bshadapar bya// de nas sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das kyi bdag nyid de
25a6(rgyud): rnams de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi gsang ba rgyan gyi bkod pa'i dkyil 'khor gyi rgyal po bka' stsal pa'i phyir/ slar yang glu'i dbyangs 'dis zhu ba zhus pa// chos dbyings mi g.yo de la
25a7(rgyud): legs bzhugs dam pa'i thugs// phyogs bcu mtha' yas sangs rgyas kyis zhabs legs btud pa// bde mchog lha yi lha ste sa dbang 'jig rten bla// dkyil 'khor bde ba mchog la bzhugs

25b1(rgyud): gzhug gsol mchod pa chen pa kye// cha lugs rnam pa du mas 'gro ldan 'dul mdzad kun gyi dam pa rtse// de nas bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyis gsol ba bta ba cing bskul ba'i tshis
25b2(rgyud): nyid kyis thugs la bzhag nas/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi dkyil 'khor bsgyur ba chen po rab tu sim pa bde ba la longs spyod pa rnam par dgyings pa rdo rje zhes bya ba'i ting 'dzin la snyems par zhugs/ 
25b3(rgyud): nas de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad byin gyis brlabs te/ bde ba chen po 'khor los bsgyur ba la rab tu gnas nas nyid kyi sku dang gsung dang thugs rdo rje rnams la rab tu phyung ngo // dkyil 'khor snga ma bzhin

25b5(rgyud): sogs pa'i rim pa yis// thams cad kun tu brtags par bya// pad+ma'i lo ma rtsibs la ni// rang gi chos dang rab tu smra la// ma mo rnams ni thams cad kyis// mchod pa la sogs rab
25b6(rgyud): tu brtag/ sgo ru sgo ba yongs su brtag/ sgo yi phyi ru sgo skyong ba// btsun mo lhan cig spyod bcas pa// kun nas lha rnams bzhag par bya// de nas rang gi sa bon gyis// klu dang gnod sbyin 'phar ma gzhan/ 
25b7(rgyud): dri za rnams dang mi 'am ci// lha min na mkha' lding de bzhin// 'jig rten skyong ba thams cad ni// sgo ru gnyis gnyis bzhag par bya// gdon dang dug dang rims dang nad// yi dgas sha ba srin po
25b8(rgyud): dang / dmyal pa brgyad po phyogs brgyad kyi// 'khor mo'i phyi ru bzhag par bya// de nas 'khor lo'i su kyang bri// chen po rin can 'dun pa bzhin// de mi ga ru br-i byab// shad du 'dod chags skyes
26a1(rgyud): / gnas lag/ zhe sdang drag po lus gnag pa// byang du legs par bri bar bya// gti mug nub tu bri bar bya// lho rung rgyal nyid yin no// sog le dang ni gos nag po// de bzhin dadrug gu/

26b1(rgyud): gyur pa// de yis sbyor bas dbang bskur bya// yang na gang 'dod rnal 'byor gyis// sbyor ba bsgoms te dbang bskur bya// yang na bdag po'i rnal 'byor gyis// gal te de ni sbyor ldan 'gyur// gdugs/

63b3(rgyud): gzugasu bskyed do// yang lha mo sgrol ma sbyor ba 'dis 'jig rten dbang phyug gi ting 'dzin gyis bsten par bya'o// de nas lha mo dgyes nas mchog gsol bar 'gyur ro// de nas lha mo de rmi lam du 'ongs te

63b8(rgyud): gal te lag pa gnyis steng du bkrol na dge bar shes par bya'o// gal te 'og tu gnas na dge ba yang ma yin mi dag ba yang ma yin par shes par bya'o// gal te rgyab tu son par gyur na mi dge ba
64a1(rgyud): / shes par bya'o// de nas bcom ldan 'das lha mo bskul byed ma sgrub par 'dod na des de'i b+ha ga'i dbus phyag na rdo rje'i skur bdag nyid bsgoms te/ de'i rtsa dang zhu ba'i sbyor ba dkar po las/

115b1(rgyud): pa'i sangs rgyas kyi zhing kun tu g.yogs nas/ chos kyi rgyal mtshan gyi tog rgya chen po yongs su dag pa'i rtse mo la lta ba zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs so// bcom ldan 'das snyoms

116a3(rgyud): chos kyi dbyings kun tu 'byung ba'i gsang sngags gsungs pa/ na maHsa man+ta bud+d+hA nAn/ d+harma d+hA t+ya swa b+hA ba At+ma ko haM/ chos kyi dbyings su byin gyis brlabs pa'o// na maHsa man+ta badz+rA nAn/ badz+ra At+ma ko ha/

116b3(rgyud): rnams ni ma mchis 'gyur// gsang sngags rnams kyang ji ltar sgrub// de yi 'bras bu ci 'drar 'gyur// de skad gsol nas de yi tshe// bcom ldan rnam snang mdzad chen gyis// 'di skad ces ni bka'/

116b8(rgyud): byas nas su// kham por gyis ni dgab par bya// kham phor ri rab chen po ru// yang dang yang du bsam par bya// de yi steng du a zhes pa// klad kor bcas pa rgyas par bsam// rlung bcing chen po de lta
117a1(rgyud): bu// sngon gyi rgyal ba rnams kyis bshad// sems dpa' chen po chu yi yang // yid gcig bsdus te mnyan par gyis// sngags pas ra zhes bya ba ni// thams cad dmar po stob
117a2(rgyud): chen bsam// 'bar ba'i phreng can mi zad pa// khro bo lag na ral gri thogs// sa la sprin gyi gzugs bris nas// ral gri phyag rgyas dbab par bya// phyogs kun nas ni langs pa'i sprin// de ma thag tu
117a3(rgyud): 'jig par 'gyur// yang na sngags pa mi g.yeng bas// de dag phur bus gdab bya ste// mkhas pa rdo rjer gyur nas su// thams cad rdo rje phur bus gdab// yang na bgegs rnams thams cad ni// zhi

120a1(rgyud): la na mo a mo g+ha nAn swA hA/ sangs rgyas dang byang chub sems dpa' thams cad kyi yum na mkha'i spyan gyi'o// de nas bcom ldan 'das rnam par snang mdzad bgegs thams cad
